 68→\t\tconfig:    config,\n    69→\t\tgitConfig: gitConfig,\n    70→\t\tclient:    client,\n    71→\t}, nil\n    72→}\n    73→\n    74→func (r *gitRepository) URL() string {\n    75→\treturn r.gitConfig.URL\n    76→}\n    77→\n    78→func (r *gitRepository) Branch() string {\n    79→\treturn r.gitConfig.Branch\n    80→}\n    81→\n    82→func (r *gitRepository) SetBranch(branch string) {\n    83→\tr.gitConfig.Branch = branch\n    84→}\n    85→\n    86→func (r *gitRepository) GetCurrentBranch() string {\n    87→\treturn r.gitConfig.Branch\n    88→}\n    89→\n    90→func (r *gitRepository) GetDefaultBranch(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {\n    91→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, \"\")\n    92→\n    93→\t// Get all refs to find the default branch\n    94→\trefs, err := r.client.ListRefs(ctx)\n    95→\tif err != nil {\n    96→\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"list refs: %w\", err)\n    97→\t}\n    98→\n    99→\tvar hasMain, hasMaster bool\n   100→\tvar firstBranch string\n   101→\n   102→\t// Single pass through refs to find main, master, or first branch alphabetically\n   103→\tfor _, ref := range refs {\n   104→\t\tif !strings.HasPrefix(ref.Name, \"refs/heads/\") {\n   105→\t\t\tcontinue\n   106→\t\t}\n   107→\n   108→\t\tbranchName := strings.TrimPrefix(ref.Name, \"refs/heads/\")\n   109→\n   110→\t\t// Check for main or master\n   111→\t\tswitch branchName {\n   112→\t\tcase \"main\":\n   113→\t\t\thasMain = true\n   114→\t\tcase \"master\":\n   115→\t\t\thasMaster = true\n   116→\t\t}\n   117→\n   118→\t\t// Track first branch alphabetically as fallback\n   119→\t\tif firstBranch == \"\" || branchName < firstBranch {\n   120→\t\t\tfirstBranch = branchName\n   121→\t\t}\n   122→\t}\n   123→\n   124→\t// No branches found\n   125→\tif firstBranch == \"\" {\n   126→\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"no branches found in repository\")\n   127→\t}\n   128→\n   129→\t// Prefer main, then master, then first branch alphabetically\n   130→\tif hasMain {\n   131→\t\treturn \"main\", nil\n   132→\t}\n   133→\tif hasMaster {\n   134→\t\treturn \"master\", nil\n   135→\t}\n   136→\n   137→\t// If neither main nor master exists, return the first branch alphabetically.\n   138→\t// This provides deterministic behavior when working with repositories that use\n   139→\t// non-standard default branch names (e.g., \"develop\", \"trunk\", custom names).\n   140→\t// Users can always change the branch afterward or specify it directly in the repository configuration.\n   141→\treturn firstBranch, nil\n   142→}\n   143→\n   144→func (r *gitRepository) Config() *provisioning.Repository {\n   145→\treturn r.config\n   146→}\n   147→\n   148→func isValidGitURL(gitURL string) bool {\n   149→\t// Parse URL\n   150→\tparsed, err := url.Parse(gitURL)\n   151→\tif err != nil {\n   152→\t\treturn false\n   153→\t}\n   154→\n   155→\t// Must be HTTPS or HTTP (HTTP allowed for local development)\n   156→\tif parsed.Scheme != \"https\" && parsed.Scheme != \"http\" {\n   157→\t\treturn false\n   158→\t}\n   159→\n   160→\t// Must have a host\n   161→\tif parsed.Host == \"\" {\n   162→\t\treturn false\n   163→\t}\n   164→\n   165→\t// Must have a path\n   166→\tif parsed.Path == \"\" || parsed.Path == \"/\" {\n   167→\t\treturn false\n   168→\t}\n   169→\n   170→\treturn true\n   171→}\n   172→\n   173→// Test implements provisioning.Repository.\n   174→func (r *gitRepository) Test(ctx context.Context) (*provisioning.TestResults, error) {\n   175→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, \"\")\n   176→\n   177→\tt := string(r.config.Spec.Type)\n   178→\n   179→\t// In case the branch is empty\n   180→\tif r.GetCurrentBranch() == \"\" {\n   181→\t\tbranch, err := r.GetDefaultBranch(ctx)\n   182→\t\tif err != nil {\n   183→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   184→\t\t}\n   185→\n   186→\t\tr.SetBranch(branch)\n   187→\t}\n   188→\n   189→\t// Check authorization\n   190→\tif ok, err := r.client.IsAuthorized(ctx); err != nil || !ok {\n   191→\t\t// Map nanogit errors to repository errors for proper HTTP status codes\n   192→\t\tif err != nil {\n   193→\t\t\terr = mapNanogitError(err)\n   194→\t\t\tif result := checkHTTPError(err, field.NewPath(\"secure\", \"token\")); result != nil {\n   195→\t\t\t\treturn result, nil\n   196→\t\t\t}\n   197→\t\t}\n   198→\n   199→\t\tdetail := \"not authorized\"\n   200→\t\tif err != nil {\n   201→\t\t\tdetail = fmt.Sprintf(\"failed check if authorized: %v\", err)\n   202→\t\t}\n   203→\n   204→\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n   205→\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n   206→\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n   207→\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n   208→\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n   209→\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"secure\", \"token\").String(),\n   210→\t\t\t\tDetail: detail,\n   211→\t\t\t}},\n   212→\t\t}, nil\n   213→\t}\n   214→\n   215→\t// Check if repository exists\n   216→\tif ok, err :=   220→\t\t\tif result := checkHTTPError(err, field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"url\")); result != nil {\n   221→\t\t\t\treturn result, nil\n   222→\t\t\t}\n   223→\t\t}\n   224→\n   225→\t\tdetail := \"repository not found\"\n   226→\t\tif err != nil {\n   227→\t\t\tdetail = fmt.Sprintf(\"failed check if repository exists: %v\", err)\n   228→\t\t}\n   229→\n   230→\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n   231→\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n   232→\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n   233→\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n   234→\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n   235→\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"url\").String(),\n   236→\t\t\t\tDetail: detail,\n   237→\t\t\t}},\n   238→\t\t}, nil\n   239→\t}\n   240→\n   241→\t// Test basic connectivity by getting the branch reference\n   242→\t_, err := r.client.GetRef(ctx, fmt.Sprintf(\"refs/heads/%s\", r.gitConfig.Branch))\n   243→\tif err != nil {\n   244→\t\t// Check for branch not found first (before mapping)\n   245→\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   246→\t\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n   247→\t\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n   248→\t\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n   249→\t\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n   250→\t\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n   251→\t\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"branch\").String(),\n   252→\t\t\t\t\tDetail: \"branch not found\",\n   253→\t\t\t\t}},\n   254→\t\t\t}, nil\n   255→\t\t}\n   256→\n   257→\t\t// Map nanogit errors to repository errors for proper HTTP status codes\n   258→\t\terr = mapNanogitError(err)\n   259→\t\tif result := checkHTTPError(err, field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"branch\")); result != nil {\n   260→\t\t\treturn result, nil\n   261→\t\t}\n   262→\n   263→\t\tdetail := fmt.Sprintf(\"failed to check if branch exists: %v\", err)\n   264→\n   265→\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n   266→\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n   267→\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n   268→\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n   269→\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n   270→\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"branch\").String(),\n   271→\t\t\t\tDetail: detail,\n   272→\t\t\t}},\n   273→\t\t}, nil\n   274→\t}\n   275→\n   276→\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n   277→\t\tCode:    http.StatusOK,\n   278→\t\tSuccess: true,\n   279→\t}, nil\n   280→}\n   281→\n   282→// Read implements provisioning.Repository.\n   283→func (r *gitRepository) Read(ctx context.Context, filePath, ref string) (*repository.FileInfo, error) {\n   284→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n   285→\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, filePath)\n   286→\n   287→\t// Resolve ref to commit hash\n   288→\trefHash, err := r.resolveRefToHash(ctx, ref)\n   289→\tif err != nil {\n   290→\t\treturn nil, err\n   291→\t}\n   292→\n   293→\t// get root hash\n   294→\t// TODO: Fix GetTree in nanogit as it does not work commit hash\n   295→\tcommit, err := r.client.GetCommit(ctx, refHash)\n   296→\tif err != nil {\n   297→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"get commit: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   298→\t}\n   299→\n   300→\t// Check if the path represents a directory\n   301→\tif safepath.IsDir(filePath) {\n   302→\t\t// Strip trailing slash for git tree lookup to avoid empty path components\n   303→\t\tfinalPath = strings.TrimSuffix(finalPath, \"/\")\n   304→\t\ttree, err := r.client.GetTreeByPath(ctx, commit.Tree, finalPath)\n   305→\t\tif err != nil {\n   306→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   307→\t\t\t\treturn nil, repository.ErrFileNotFound\n   308→\t\t\t}\n   309→\n   310→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"get tree by path: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   311→\t\t}\n   312→\n   313→\t\treturn &repository.FileInfo{\n   314→\t\t\tPath: filePath,\n   315→\t\t\tRef:  refHash.String(),\n   316→\t\t\tHash: tree.Hash.String(),\n   317→\t\t}, nil\n   318→\t}\n   319→\n   320→\tblob, err := r.client.GetBlobByPath(ctx, commit.Tree, finalPath)\n   321→\tif err != nil {\n   322→\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   323→\t\t\treturn nil, repository.ErrFileNotFound\n   324→\t\t}\n   325→\n   326→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"read blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   327→\t}\n   328→\n   329→\treturn &repository.FileInfo{\n   330→\t\tPath: filePath,\n   331→\t\tRef:  ref,\n   332→\t\tData: blob.Content,\n   333→\t\tHash: blob.Hash.String(),\n   334→\t}, nil\n   335→}\n   336→\n   337→func (r *gitRepository) ReadTree(ctx context.Context, ref string) ([]repository.FileTreeEntry, error) {\n   338→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n   339→\n   340→\t// Resolve ref to commit hash\n   341→\trefHash, err := r.resolveRefToHash(ctx, ref)\n   342→\tif err != nil {\n   343→\t\treturn nil, err\n   344→\t}\n   345→\n   346→\t// Get flat tree using nanogit's GetFlatTree\n   347→\ttree, err := r.client.GetFlatTree(ctx, refHash)\n   348→\tif err != nil {\n   349→\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   350→\t\t\treturn nil, repository.ErrRefNotFound\n   351→\t\t}\n   352→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"get flat tree: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   353→\t}\n   354→\n   355→\tentries := make([]repository.FileTreeEntry, 0, len(tree.Entries))\n   356→\tfor _, entry := range tree.Entries {\n   357→\t\tisBlob := entry.Type == protocol.ObjectTypeBlob\n   358→\t\t// Apply path prefix filtering\n   359→\t\trelativePath, err := safepath.RelativeTo(entry.Path, r.gitConfig.Path)\n   360→\t\tif err != nil {\n   361→\t\t\t// File is outside configured path, skip it\n   362→\t\t\tcontinue\n   363→\t\t}\n   364→\n   365→\t\tfilePath := relativePath\n   366→\t\tif !isBlob && !safepath.IsDir(filePath) {\n   367→\t\t\tfilePath = filePath + \"/\"\n   368→\t\t}\n   369→\n   370→\t\tconverted := repository.FileTreeEntry{\n   371→\t\t\tPath: filePath,\n   372→\t\t\t// TODO: Remove size from repository.FileTreeEntry. We don't need it per se.\n   373→\t\t\tSize: 0, // FlatTreeEntry doesn't have size, set to 0\n   374→\t\t\tHash: entry.Hash.String(),\n   375→\t\t\tBlob: isBlob,\n   376→\t\t}\n   377→\t\tentries = append(entries, converted)\n   378→\t}\n   379→\treturn entries, nil\n   380→}\n   381→\n   382→func (r *gitRepository) Create(ctx context.Context, path, ref string, data []byte, comment string) error {\n   383→\tif ref == \"\" {\n   384→\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n   385→\t}\n   386→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n   387→\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n   388→\tif err != nil {\n   389→\t\treturn err\n   390→\t}\n   391→\n   392→\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n   393→\tif err != nil {\n   394→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   395→\t}\n   396→\n   397→\tif err := r.create(ctx, path, data, writer); err != nil {\n   398→\t\treturn err\n   399→\t}\n   400→\n   401→\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n   402→}\n   403→\n   404→func (r *gitRepository) create(ctx context.Context, path string, data []byte, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n   405→\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, path)\n   406→\t// Create .keep file if it is a directory\n   407→\tif safepath.IsDir(finalPath) {\n   408→\t\tif data != nil {\n   409→\t\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"data cannot be provided for a directory\")\n   410→\t\t}\n   411→\n   412→\t\tfinalPath = safepath.Join(finalPath, \".keep\")\n   413→\t\tdata = []byte{}\n   414→\t}\n   415→\n   416→\tif _, err := writer.CreateBlob(ctx, finalPath, data); err != nil {\n   417→\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectAlreadyExists) {\n   418→\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileAlreadyExists\n   419→\t\t}\n   420→\n   421→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   422→\t}\n   423→\n   424→\treturn nil\n   425→}\n   426→\n   427→func (r *gitRepository) Update(ctx context.Context, path, ref string, data []byte, comment string) error {\n   428→\tif ref == \"\" {\n   429→\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n   430→\t}\n   431→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n   432→\n   433→\t// Check if trying to update a directory\n   434→\tif safepath.IsDir(path) {\n   435→\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"cannot update a directory\")\n   436→\t}\n   437→\n   438→\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n   439→\tif err != nil {\n   440→\t\treturn err\n   441→\t}\n   442→\t// Create a staged writer\n   443→\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n   444→\tif err != nil {\n   445→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   446→\t}\n   447→\n   448→\tif err := r.update(ctx, path, data, writer); err != nil {\n   449→\t\treturn err\n   450→\t}\n   451→\n   452→\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n   453→}\n   454→\n   455→func (r *gitRepository) update(ctx context.Context, path string, data []byte, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n   456→\t// Check if trying to update a directory\n   457→\tif safepath.IsDir(path) {\n   458→\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"cannot update a directory\")\n   459→\t}\n   460→\n   461→\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, path)\n   462→\tif _, err := writer.UpdateBlob(ctx, finalPath, data); err != nil {\n   463→\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   464→\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n   465→\t\t}\n   466→\n   467→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"update blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   468→\t}\n   469→\n   470→\treturn nil\n   471→}\n   472→\n   473→func (r *gitRepository) Write(ctx context.Context, path string, ref string, data []byte, message string) error {\n   474→\tif ref == \"\" {\n   475→\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n   476→\t}\n   477→\n   478→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n   479→\tinfo, err := r.Read(ctx, path, ref)\n   480→\tif err != nil && !(errors.Is(err, repository.ErrFileNotFound)) {\n   481→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"check if file exists before writing: %w\", err)\n   482→\t}\n   483→\tif err == nil {\n   484→\t\t// If the value already exists and is the same, we don't need to do anything\n   485→\t\tif bytes.Equal(info.Data, data) {\n   486→\t\t\treturn nil\n   487→\t\t}\n   488→\t\treturn r.Update(ctx, path, ref, data, message)\n   489→\t}\n   490→\n   491→\treturn r.Create(ctx, path, ref, data, message)\n   492→}\n   493→\n   494→func (r *gitRepository) Delete(ctx context.Context, path, ref, comment string) error {\n   495→\tif ref == \"\" {\n   496→\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n   497→\t}\n   498→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n   499→\n   500→\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n   501→\tif err != nil {\n   502→\t\treturn err\n   503→\t}\n   504→\t// Create a staged writer\n   505→\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n   506→\tif err != nil {\n   507→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   508→\t}\n   509→\n   510→\tif err := r.delete(ctx, path, writer); err != nil {\n   511→\t\treturn err\n   512→\t}\n   513→\n   514→\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n   515→}\n   516→\n   517→func (r *gitRepository) Move(ctx context.Context, oldPath, newPath, ref, comment string) error {\n   518→\tif ref == \"\" {\n   519→\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n   520→\t}\n   521→\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n   522→\n   523→\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n   524→\tif err != nil {\n   525→\t\treturn err\n   526→\t}\n   527→\n   528→\t// Create a staged writer\n   529→\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n   530→\tif err != nil {\n   531→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   532→\t}\n   533→\n   534→\tif err := r.move(ctx, oldPath, newPath, writer); err != nil {\n   535→\t\treturn err\n   536→\t}\n   537→\n   538→\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n   539→}\n   540→\n   541→func (r *gitRepository) delete(ctx context.Context, path string, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n   542→\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, path)\n   543→\t// Check if it's a directory - use DeleteTree for directories, DeleteBlob for files\n   544→\tif safepath.IsDir(path) {\n   545→\t\ttrimmed := strings.TrimSuffix(finalPath, \"/\")\n   546→\t\tif _, err := writer.DeleteTree(ctx, trimmed); err != nil {\n   547→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   548→\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n   549→\t\t\t}\n   550→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete tree: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   551→\t\t}\n   552→\t} else {\n   553→\t\tif _, err := writer.DeleteBlob(ctx, finalPath); err != nil {\n   554→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   555→\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n   556→\t\t\t}\n   557→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   558→\t\t}\n   559→\t}\n   560→\n   561→\treturn nil\n   562→}\n   563→\n   564→func (r *gitRepository) move(ctx context.Context, oldPath, newPath string, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n   565→\toldFinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, oldPath)\n   566→\tnewFinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, newPath)\n   567→\n   568→\t// Check if moving directories\n   569→\tif safepath.IsDir(oldPath) && safepath.IsDir(newPath) {\n   570→\t\t// For directories, trim trailing slashes and use MoveTree\n   571→\t\toldTrimmed := strings.TrimSuffix(oldFinalPath, \"/\")\n   572→\t\tnewTrimmed := strings.TrimSuffix(newFinalPath, \"/\")\n   573→\n   574→\t\tif _, err := writer.MoveTree(ctx, oldTrimmed, newTrimmed); err != nil {\n   575→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   576→\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n   577→\t\t\t}\n   578→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectAlreadyExists) {\n   579→\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileAlreadyExists\n   580→\t\t\t}\n   581→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"move tree: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   582→\t\t}\n   583→\t} else if !safepath.IsDir(oldPath) && !safepath.IsDir(newPath) {\n   584→\t\t// For files, use MoveBlob operation\n   585→\t\tif _, err := writer.MoveBlob(ctx, oldFinalPath, newFinalPath); err != nil {\n   586→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n   587→\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n   588→\t\t\t}\n   589→\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectAlreadyExists) {\n   590→\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileAlreadyExists\n   591→\t\t\t}\n   592→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"move blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n   593→\t\t}\n   594→\t} else {\n   595→\t\t// Mismatched types (file to directory or vice versa)\n   596→\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"cannot move between file and directory types\")\n   597→\t}\n   598→\n   599→\treturn nil\n   600→}\n   601→\n   602→func (r when:\n   879→//   - Network errors occur: connection timeouts, temporary network failures, or connection errors\n   880→//   - HTTP 5xx server errors: For GET and DELETE operations (idempotent)\n   881→//   - HTTP 429 Too Many Requests: For all operations (rate limiting is temporary)\n   882→//\n   883→// The retry behavior:\n   884→//   - Total attempts: 8 (1 initial attempt + 7 retries)\n   885→//   - Initial delay: 100ms before the first retry\n   886→//   - Exponential backoff: delay doubles after each failed attempt (100ms → 200ms → 400ms → 800ms → 1.6s → 3.2s → 5s)\n   887→//   - Maximum delay: capped at 5 seconds\n   888→//   - Jitter: enabled to prevent thundering herd problems\n   889→//   - Total retry window: approximately 10 seconds from first attempt to last retry\n   890→//\n   891→// All attempts will fail when:\n   892→//   - The Git server is completely unavailable or unreachable\n   893→//   - Network connectivity issues persist beyond the retry window (~10 seconds)\n   894→//   - The server returns transient errors consistently for the entire retry duration\n   895→//   - Context cancellation occurs before retries complete\n   896→//\n   897→// Non-transient errors (e.g., 4xx client errors except 429, authentication failures) are not retried and returned immediately.\n   898→func defaultGitRetrier() *retry.ExponentialBackoffRetrier {\n   899→\treturn retry.NewExponentialBackoffRetrier().\n   900→\t\tWithMaxAttempts(8). // 1 initial + 7 retries = 8 total attempts (~10s total retry window)\n   901→\t\tWithInitialDelay(100 * time.Millisecond).\n   902→\t\tWithMaxDelay(5 * time.Second).\n   903→\t\tWithMultiplier(2.0).\n   904→\t\tWithJitter()\n   905→}\n   906→\n   907→// ensureRetryContext ensures that retry logic is configured in the context.\n   908→// This function should be called at the beginning of all methods that make client calls\n   909→// to guarantee retry logic is always present, regardless of context state.\n   910→func ensureRetryContext(ctx context.Context) context.Context {\n   911→\t// Only add retrier if one doesn't already exist in the context\n   912→\tif retry.FromContext(ctx).MaxAttempts() <= 1 {\n   913→\t\tctx = retry.ToContext(ctx, defaultGitRetrier())\n   914→\t}\n   915→\treturn ctx\n   916→}\n   917→\n   918→// withGitContext sets up the context with logging, git repository metadata, and retry logic.\n   919→// This function should be called at the beginning of all public methods to ensure:\n   920→// - Proper logging context with git repository details\n   921→// - Retry logic is configured for all Git operations\n   922→// - Context is properly prepared for nanogit client calls\n   923→func (r *gitRepository) withGitContext(ctx Single pass through refs to find main, master, or first branch alphabetically\n\tfor _, ref := range refs {\n\t\tif !strings.HasPrefix(ref.Name, \"refs/heads/\") {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbranchName := strings.TrimPrefix(ref.Name, \"refs/heads/\")\n\n\t\t// Check for main or master\n\t\tswitch branchName {\n\t\tcase \"main\":\n\t\t\thasMain = true\n\t\tcase \"master\":\n\t\t\thasMaster = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Track first branch alphabetically as fallback\n\t\tif firstBranch == \"\" || branchName < firstBranch {\n\t\t\tfirstBranch = branchName\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// No branches found\n\tif firstBranch == \"\" {\n\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"no branches found in repository\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Prefer main, then master, then first branch alphabetically\n\tif hasMain {\n\t\treturn \"main\", nil\n\t}\n\tif hasMaster {\n\t\treturn \"master\", nil\n\t}\n\n\t// If neither main nor master exists, return the first branch alphabetically.\n\t// This provides deterministic behavior when working with repositories that use\n\t// non-standard default branch names (e.g., \"develop\", \"trunk\", custom names).\n\t// Users can always change the branch afterward or specify it directly in the repository configuration.\n\treturn firstBranch, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Config() *provisioning.Repository {\n\treturn r.config\n}\n\nfunc isValidGitURL(gitURL string) bool {\n\t// Parse URL\n\tparsed, err := url.Parse(gitURL)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// Must be HTTPS or HTTP (HTTP allowed for local development)\n\tif parsed.Scheme != \"https\" && parsed.Scheme != \"http\" {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// Must have a host\n\tif parsed.Host == \"\" {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\t// Must have a path\n\tif parsed.Path == \"\" || parsed.Path == \"/\" {\n\t\treturn false\n\t}\n\n\treturn true\n}\n\n// Test implements provisioning.Repository.\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Test(ctx context.Context) (*provisioning.TestResults, error) {\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, \"\")\n\n\tt := string(r.config.Spec.Type)\n\n\t// In case the branch is empty\n\tif r.GetCurrentBranch() == \"\" {\n\t\tbranch, err := r.GetDefaultBranch(ctx)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, err\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tr.SetBranch(branch)\n\t}\n\n\t// Check authorization\n\tif ok, err := r.client.IsAuthorized(ctx); err != nil || !ok {\n\t\t// Map nanogit errors to repository errors for proper HTTP status codes\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terr = mapNanogitError(err)\n\t\t\tif result := checkHTTPError(err, field.NewPath(\"secure\", \"token\")); result != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn result, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tdetail := \"not authorized\"\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tdetail = fmt.Sprintf(\"failed check if authorized: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"secure\", \"token\").String(),\n\t\t\t\tDetail: detail,\n\t\t\t}},\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if repository exists\n\tif ok, err := r.client.RepoExists(ctx); err != nil || !ok {\n\t\t// Map nanogit errors to repository errors for proper HTTP status codes\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\terr = mapNanogitError(err)\n\t\t\tif result := checkHTTPError(err, field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"url\")); result != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn result, nil\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tdetail := \"repository not found\"\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tdetail = fmt.Sprintf(\"failed check if repository exists: %v\", err)\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"url\").String(),\n\t\t\t\tDetail: detail,\n\t\t\t}},\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Test basic connectivity by getting the branch reference\n\t_, err := r.client.GetRef(ctx, fmt.Sprintf(\"refs/heads/%s\", r.gitConfig.Branch))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// Check for branch not found first (before mapping)\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n\t\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n\t\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n\t\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n\t\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"branch\").String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDetail: \"branch not found\",\n\t\t\t\t}},\n\t\t\t}, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Map nanogit errors to repository errors for proper HTTP status codes\n\t\terr = mapNanogitError(err)\n\t\tif result := checkHTTPError(err, field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"branch\")); result != nil {\n\t\t\treturn result, nil\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tdetail := fmt.Sprintf(\"failed to check if branch exists: %v\", err)\n\n\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"spec\", t, \"branch\").String(),\n\t\t\t\tDetail: detail,\n\t\t\t}},\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\tCode:    http.StatusOK,\n\t\tSuccess: true,\n\t}, nil\n}\n\n// Read implements provisioning.Repository.\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Read(ctx context.Context, filePath, ref string) (*repository.FileInfo, error) {\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, filePath)\n\n\t// Resolve ref to commit hash\n\trefHash, err := r.resolveRefToHash(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\t// get root hash\n\t// TODO: Fix GetTree in nanogit as it does not work commit hash\n\tcommit, err := r.client.GetCommit(ctx, refHash)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"get commit: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if the path represents a directory\n\tif safepath.IsDir(filePath) {\n\t\t// Strip trailing slash for git tree lookup to avoid empty path components\n\t\tfinalPath = strings.TrimSuffix(finalPath, \"/\")\n\t\ttree, err := r.client.GetTreeByPath(ctx, commit.Tree, finalPath)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\t\treturn nil, repository.ErrFileNotFound\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"get tree by path: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn &repository.FileInfo{\n\t\t\tPath: filePath,\n\t\t\tRef:  refHash.String(),\n\t\t\tHash: tree.Hash.String(),\n\t\t}, nil\n\t}\n\n\tblob, err := r.client.GetBlobByPath(ctx, commit.Tree, finalPath)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\treturn nil, repository.ErrFileNotFound\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"read blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\treturn &repository.FileInfo{\n\t\tPath: filePath,\n\t\tRef:  ref,\n\t\tData: blob.Content,\n\t\tHash: blob.Hash.String(),\n\t}, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) ReadTree(ctx context.Context, ref string) ([]repository.FileTreeEntry, error) {\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\n\t// Resolve ref to commit hash\n\trefHash, err := r.resolveRefToHash(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, err\n\t}\n\n\t// Get flat tree using nanogit's GetFlatTree\n\ttree, err := r.client.GetFlatTree(ctx, refHash)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\treturn nil, repository.ErrRefNotFound\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"get flat tree: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\tentries := make([]repository.FileTreeEntry, 0, len(tree.Entries))\n\tfor _, entry := range tree.Entries {\n\t\tisBlob := entry.Type == protocol.ObjectTypeBlob\n\t\t// Apply path prefix filtering\n\t\trelativePath, err := safepath.RelativeTo(entry.Path, r.gitConfig.Path)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t// File is outside configured path, skip it\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfilePath := relativePath\n\t\tif !isBlob && !safepath.IsDir(filePath) {\n\t\t\tfilePath = filePath + \"/\"\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tconverted := repository.FileTreeEntry{\n\t\t\tPath: filePath,\n\t\t\t// TODO: Remove size from repository.FileTreeEntry. We don't need it per se.\n\t\t\tSize: 0, // FlatTreeEntry doesn't have size, set to 0\n\t\t\tHash: entry.Hash.String(),\n\t\t\tBlob: isBlob,\n\t\t}\n\t\tentries = append(entries, converted)\n\t}\n\treturn entries, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Create(ctx context.Context, path, ref string, data []byte, comment string) error {\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n\t}\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\tif err := r.create(ctx, path, data, writer); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) create(ctx context.Context, path string, data []byte, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, path)\n\t// Create .keep file if it is a directory\n\tif safepath.IsDir(finalPath) {\n\t\tif data != nil {\n\t\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"data cannot be provided for a directory\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tfinalPath = safepath.Join(finalPath, \".keep\")\n\t\tdata = []byte{}\n\t}\n\n\tif _, err := writer.CreateBlob(ctx, finalPath, data); err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectAlreadyExists) {\n\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileAlreadyExists\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Update(ctx context.Context, path, ref string, data []byte, comment string) error {\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n\t}\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\n\t// Check if trying to update a directory\n\tif safepath.IsDir(path) {\n\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"cannot update a directory\")\n\t}\n\n\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\t// Create a staged writer\n\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\tif err := r.update(ctx, path, data, writer); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) update(ctx context.Context, path string, data []byte, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n\t// Check if trying to update a directory\n\tif safepath.IsDir(path) {\n\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"cannot update a directory\")\n\t}\n\n\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, path)\n\tif _, err := writer.UpdateBlob(ctx, finalPath, data); err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"update blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Write(ctx context.Context, path string, ref string, data []byte, message string) error {\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n\t}\n\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\tinfo, err := r.Read(ctx, path, ref)\n\tif err != nil && !(errors.Is(err, repository.ErrFileNotFound)) {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"check if file exists before writing: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\t// If the value already exists and is the same, we don't need to do anything\n\t\tif bytes.Equal(info.Data, data) {\n\t\t\treturn nil\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn r.Update(ctx, path, ref, data, message)\n\t}\n\n\treturn r.Create(ctx, path, ref, data, message)\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Delete(ctx context.Context, path, ref, comment string) error {\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n\t}\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\n\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\t// Create a staged writer\n\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\tif err := r.delete(ctx, path, writer); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Move(ctx context.Context, oldPath, newPath, ref, comment string) error {\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n\t}\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\n\tbranchRef, err := r.ensureBranchExists(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\t// Create a staged writer\n\twriter, err := r.client.NewStagedWriter(ctx, branchRef)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create staged writer: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\tif err := r.move(ctx, oldPath, newPath, writer); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\treturn r.commitAndPush(ctx, writer, comment)\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) delete(ctx context.Context, path string, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n\tfinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, path)\n\t// Check if it's a directory - use DeleteTree for directories, DeleteBlob for files\n\tif safepath.IsDir(path) {\n\t\ttrimmed := strings.TrimSuffix(finalPath, \"/\")\n\t\tif _, err := writer.DeleteTree(ctx, trimmed); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete tree: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\tif _, err := writer.DeleteBlob(ctx, finalPath); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) move(ctx context.Context, oldPath, newPath string, writer nanogit.StagedWriter) error {\n\toldFinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, oldPath)\n\tnewFinalPath := safepath.Join(r.gitConfig.Path, newPath)\n\n\t// Check if moving directories\n\tif safepath.IsDir(oldPath) && safepath.IsDir(newPath) {\n\t\t// For directories, trim trailing slashes and use MoveTree\n\t\toldTrimmed := strings.TrimSuffix(oldFinalPath, \"/\")\n\t\tnewTrimmed := strings.TrimSuffix(newFinalPath, \"/\")\n\n\t\tif _, err := writer.MoveTree(ctx, oldTrimmed, newTrimmed); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectAlreadyExists) {\n\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileAlreadyExists\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"move tree: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t\t}\n\t} else if !safepath.IsDir(oldPath) && !safepath.IsDir(newPath) {\n\t\t// For files, use MoveBlob operation\n\t\tif _, err := writer.MoveBlob(ctx, oldFinalPath, newFinalPath); err != nil {\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileNotFound\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectAlreadyExists) {\n\t\t\t\treturn repository.ErrFileAlreadyExists\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"move blob: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t\t}\n\t} else {\n\t\t// Mismatched types (file to directory or vice versa)\n\t\treturn apierrors.NewBadRequest(\"cannot move between file and directory types\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) History(_ context.Context, _ string, _ string) ([]provisioning.HistoryItem, error) {\n\treturn nil, &apierrors.StatusError{ErrStatus: metav1.Status{\n\t\tStatus:  metav1.StatusFailure,\n\t\tCode:    http.StatusNotImplemented,\n\t\tReason:  metav1.StatusReasonMethodNotAllowed,\n\t\tMessage: \"history is not supported for pure git repositories\",\n\t}}\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) ListRefs(ctx context.Context) ([]provisioning.RefItem, error) {\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, \"\")\n\trefs, err := r.client.ListRefs(ctx)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"list refs: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\trefItems := make([]provisioning.RefItem, 0, len(refs))\n\tfor _, ref := range refs {\n\t\t// Only branches\n\t\tif !strings.HasPrefix(ref.Name, \"refs/heads/\") {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\trefItems = append(refItems, provisioning.RefItem{\n\t\t\tName: strings.TrimPrefix(ref.Name, \"refs/heads/\"),\n\t\t\tHash: ref.Hash.String(),\n\t\t})\n\t}\n\n\treturn refItems, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) LatestRef(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, \"\")\n\tbranchRef, err := r.client.GetRef(ctx, fmt.Sprintf(\"refs/heads/%s\", r.gitConfig.Branch))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn \"\", fmt.Errorf(\"get branch ref: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\treturn branchRef.Hash.String(), nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) CompareFiles(ctx context.Context, base, ref string) ([]repository.VersionedFileChange, error) {\n\tif base == \"\" && ref == \"\" {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"base and ref cannot be empty\")\n\t}\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"ref cannot be empty\")\n\t}\n\n\tctx, logger := r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\n\t// Resolve base ref to hash\n\tvar baseHash hash.Hash\n\tif base != \"\" {\n\t\tvar err error\n\t\tbaseHash, err = r.resolveRefToHash(ctx, base)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"resolve base ref: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Resolve ref to hash\n\trefHash, err := r.resolveRefToHash(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"resolve ref: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Get commit hashes for base and ref\n\t// Compare commits using nanogit\n\tfiles, err := r.client.CompareCommits(ctx, baseHash, refHash)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"compare commits: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\tchanges := make([]repository.VersionedFileChange, 0)\n\tfor _, f := range files {\n\t\tswitch f.Status {\n\t\tcase protocol.FileStatusAdded:\n\t\t\tcurrentPath, err := safepath.RelativeTo(f.Path, r.gitConfig.Path)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t// do nothing as it's outside of configured path\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tchanges = append(changes, repository.VersionedFileChange{\n\t\t\t\tPath:   currentPath,\n\t\t\t\tRef:    ref,\n\t\t\t\tAction: repository.FileActionCreated,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tcase protocol.FileStatusModified:\n\t\t\tcurrentPath, err := safepath.RelativeTo(f.Path, r.gitConfig.Path)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t// do nothing as it's outside of configured path\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tchanges = append(changes, repository.VersionedFileChange{\n\t\t\t\tPath:   currentPath,\n\t\t\t\tRef:    ref,\n\t\t\t\tAction: repository.FileActionUpdated,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tcase protocol.FileStatusDeleted:\n\t\t\tcurrentPath, err := safepath.RelativeTo(f.Path, r.gitConfig.Path)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t// do nothing as it's outside of configured path\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tchanges = append(changes, repository.VersionedFileChange{\n\t\t\t\tRef:          ref,\n\t\t\t\tPreviousRef:  base,\n\t\t\t\tPath:         currentPath,\n\t\t\t\tPreviousPath: currentPath,\n\t\t\t\tAction:       repository.FileActionDeleted,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tcase protocol.FileStatusTypeChanged:\n\t\t\t// Handle type changes as modifications\n\t\t\tcurrentPath, err := safepath.RelativeTo(f.Path, r.gitConfig.Path)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t// do nothing as it's outside of configured path\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tchanges = append(changes, repository.VersionedFileChange{\n\t\t\t\tPath:   currentPath,\n\t\t\t\tRef:    ref,\n\t\t\t\tAction: repository.FileActionUpdated,\n\t\t\t})\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\tlogger.Error(\"ignore unhandled file\", \"file\", f.Path, \"status\", string(f.Status))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn changes, nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) Stage(ctx context.Context, opts repository.StageOptions) (repository.StagedRepository, error) {\n\tctx = ensureRetryContext(ctx)\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, \"\")\n\treturn NewStagedGitRepository(ctx, r, opts)\n}\n\n// resolveRefToHash resolves a ref (branch name or commit hash) to a commit hash\nfunc (r *gitRepository) resolveRefToHash(ctx context.Context, ref string) (hash.Hash, error) {\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, ref)\n\n\t// Use default branch if ref is empty\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\tref = r.gitConfig.Branch\n\t}\n\n\t// Try to parse ref as a hash first\n\trefHash, err := hash.FromHex(ref)\n\tif err == nil && refHash != hash.Zero {\n\t\t// Valid hash, return it\n\t\treturn refHash, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Prefix ref with refs/heads/\n\tref = fmt.Sprintf(\"refs/heads/%s\", ref)\n\n\t// Not a valid hash, try to resolve as a branch reference\n\tbranchRef, err := r.client.GetRef(ctx, ref)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\t\treturn hash.Zero, fmt.Errorf(\"ref not found: %s: %w\", ref, repository.ErrRefNotFound)\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn hash.Zero, fmt.Errorf(\"get ref %s: %w\", ref, mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\treturn branchRef.Hash, nil\n}\n\n// ensureBranchExists checks if a branch exists and creates it if it doesn't,\n// returning the branch reference to avoid duplicate GetRef calls\nfunc (r *gitRepository) ensureBranchExists(ctx context.Context, branchName string) (nanogit.Ref, error) {\n\tctx, _ = r.withGitContext(ctx, branchName)\n\n\tif !IsValidGitBranchName(branchName) {\n\t\treturn nanogit.Ref{}, &apierrors.StatusError{\n\t\t\tErrStatus: metav1.Status{\n\t\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusBadRequest,\n\t\t\t\tMessage: \"invalid branch name\",\n\t\t\t},\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Check if branch exists by trying to get the branch reference\n\tbranchRef, err := r.client.GetRef(ctx, fmt.Sprintf(\"refs/heads/%s\", branchName))\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\t// Branch exists, return it\n\t\tlogging.FromContext(ctx).Info(\"branch already exists\", \"branch\", branchName)\n\t\treturn branchRef, nil\n\t}\n\n\t// If error is not \"ref not found\", return the error\n\tif !errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrObjectNotFound) {\n\t\treturn nanogit.Ref{}, fmt.Errorf(\"check branch exists: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\n\t// Branch doesn't exist, create it based on the configured branch\n\tsrcBranch := r.gitConfig.Branch\n\tsrcRef, err := r.client.GetRef(ctx, fmt.Sprintf(\"refs/heads/%s\", srcBranch))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nanogit.Ref{}, fmt.Errorf(\"get signatures using the context signature if available,\n// falling back to default Grafana signature\nfunc (r *gitRepository) createSignature(ctx context.Context) (nanogit.Author, nanogit.Committer) {\n\tauthor := nanogit.Author{\n\t\tName:  \"Grafana\",\n\t\tEmail: \"noreply@grafana.com\",\n\t\tTime:  time.Now(),\n\t}\n\n\t// Use signature from context if available\n\tif sig := repository.GetAuthorSignature(ctx); sig != nil {\n\t\tif sig.Name != \"\" {\n\t\t\tauthor.Name = sig.Name\n\t\t}\n\t\tif sig.Email != \"\" {\n\t\t\tauthor.Email = sig.Email\n\t\t}\n\t\tif !sig.When.IsZero() {\n\t\t\tauthor.Time = sig.When\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif author.Time.IsZero() {\n\t\tauthor.Time = time.Now()\n\t}\n\n\t// Author and committer are always the same (for now)\n\treturn author, nanogit.Committer(author)\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) commit(ctx context.Context, writer nanogit.StagedWriter, comment string) error {\n\tauthor, committer := r.createSignature(ctx)\n\tif _, err := writer.Commit(ctx, comment, author, committer); err != nil {\n\t\tif errors.Is(err, nanogit.ErrNothingToCommit) {\n\t\t\treturn repository.ErrNothingToCommit\n\t\t}\n\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"commit changes: %w\", err)\n\t}\n\treturn nil\n}\n\nfunc (r *gitRepository) commitAndPush(ctx context.Context, writer nanogit.StagedWriter, comment string) error {\n\tif err := r.commit(ctx, writer, comment); err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tif err := writer.Push(ctx); err != nil {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"push changes: %w\", mapNanogitError(err))\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n\n// defaultGitRetrier returns a default retrier configuration for Git operations.\n//\n// Retry attempts will happen when:\n//   - Network errors occur: connection timeouts, temporary network failures, or connection errors\n//   - HTTP 5xx server errors: For GET and DELETE operations (idempotent)\n//   - HTTP 429 Too Many Requests: For all operations (rate limiting is temporary)\n//\n// The retry behavior:\n//   - Total attempts: 8 (1 initial attempt + 7 retries)\n//   - Initial delay: 100ms before the first retry\n//   - Exponential backoff: delay doubles after each failed attempt (100ms → 200ms → 400ms → 800ms → 1.6s → 3.2s → 5s)\n//   - Maximum delay: capped at 5 seconds\n//   - Jitter: enabled to prevent thundering herd problems\n//   - Total retry window: approximately 10 seconds from first attempt to last retry\n//\n// All attempts will fail when:\n//   - The Git server is completely unavailable or unreachable\n//   - Network connectivity issues persist beyond the retry window (~10 seconds)\n//   - The server returns transient errors consistently for the entire retry duration\n//   - Context cancellation occurs before retries complete\n//\n// Non-transient errors (e.g., 4xx client errors except 429, authentication failures) are not retried and returned immediately.\nfunc defaultGitRetrier() *retry.ExponentialBackoffRetrier {\n\treturn retry.NewExponentialBackoffRetrier().\n\t\tWithMaxAttempts(8). // 1 initial + 7 retries = 8 total attempts (~10s total retry window)\n\t\tWithInitialDelay(100 * time.Millisecond).\n\t\tWithMaxDelay(5 * time.Second).\n\t\tWithMultiplier(2.0).\n\t\tWithJitter()\n}\n\n// ensureRetryContext ensures that retry logic is configured in the context.\n// This function should be called at the beginning of all methods that make client calls\n// to guarantee retry logic is always present, regardless of context state.\nfunc ensureRetryContext(ctx context.Context) context.Context {\n\t// Only add retrier if one doesn't already exist in the context\n\tif retry.FromContext(ctx).MaxAttempts() <= 1 {\n\t\tctx = retry.ToContext(ctx, defaultGitRetrier())\n\t}\n\treturn ctx\n}\n\n// withGitContext sets up the context with logging, git repository metadata, and retry logic.\n// This function should be called at the beginning of all public methods to ensure:\n// - Proper logging context with git repository details\n// - Retry logic is configured for all Git operations\n// - Context is properly prepared for nanogit client calls\nfunc (r *gitRepository) withGitContext(ctx context.Context, ref string) (context.Context, logging.Logger) {\n\t// Ensure retry logic is configured first, before any early returns\n\tctx = ensureRetryContext(ctx)\n\n\tlogger := logging.FromContext(ctx)\n\n\ttype containsGit int\n\tvar containsGitKey containsGit\n\tif ctx.Value(containsGitKey) != nil {\n\t\treturn ctx, logging.FromContext(ctx)\n\t}\n\n\tif ref == \"\" {\n\t\tref = we don't add multiple git_repository keys. With doesn't deduplicate the keys...\n\tctx = context.WithValue(ctx, containsGitKey, true)\n\n\tctx = log.ToContext(ctx, logger)\n\n\treturn ctx, logger\n}\n\n// mapNanogitError converts nanogit-specific errors to repository errors.\n// This maintains the abstraction boundary and allows proper HTTP status code handling.\nfunc mapNanogitError(err error) error {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\t// Map structured nanogit errors to repository errors using the sentinel errors\n\t// from the client package (nanogit re-exports error types but not sentinel errors)\n\tif errors.Is(err, client.ErrUnauthorized) {\n\t\treturn repository.ErrUnauthorized\n\t}\n\tif errors.Is(err, client.ErrPermissionDenied) {\n\t\treturn repository.ErrPermissionDenied\n\t}\n\tif errors.Is(err, client.ErrServerUnavailable) {\n\t\treturn repository.ErrServerUnavailable\n\t}\n\n\t// Return original error if not a known nanogit error\n\treturn err\n}\n\n// checkHTTPError checks if the error is a known HTTP error (401, 403, 503) and returns\n// the appropriate TestResults. Returns nil if the error is not a known HTTP error.\nfunc checkHTTPError(err error, fieldPath *field.Path) *provisioning.TestResults {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, repository.ErrUnauthorized) {\n\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusUnauthorized,\n\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"secure\", \"token\").String(),\n\t\t\t\tDetail: \"authentication failed\",\n\t\t\t}},\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, repository.ErrPermissionDenied) {\n\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusForbidden,\n\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n\t\t\t\tField:  field.NewPath(\"secure\", \"token\").String(),\n\t\t\t\tDetail: \"permission denied\",\n\t\t\t}},\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, repository.ErrServerUnavailable) {\n\t\treturn &provisioning.TestResults{\n\t\t\tCode:    http.StatusServiceUnavailable,\n\t\t\tSuccess: false,\n\t\t\tErrors: []provisioning.ErrorDetails{{\n\t\t\t\tType:   metav1.CauseTypeFieldValueInvalid,\n\t\t\t\tField:  fieldPath.String(),\n\t\t\t\tDetail: fmt.Sprintf(\"server unavailable: %v\", err),\n\t\t\t}},\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn nil\n}\n","numLines":1016,"startLine":1,"totalLines":1016}}}

If not positive, the duration is not\n    45→\t// changed. Used for exponential backoff in combination with\n    46→\t// Factor and Cap.\n    47→\tSteps int\n    48→\t// A limit on revised values of the duration parameter. If a\n    49→\t// multiplication by the factor parameter would make the duration\n    50→\t// exceed the cap then the duration is set to the cap and the\n    51→\t// steps parameter is set to zero.\n    52→\tCap time.Duration\n    53→}\n    54→\n    55→// Step returns an amount of time to sleep determined by the original\n    56→// Duration and Jitter. The backoff is mutated to update its Steps and\n    57→// Duration. A nil Backoff always has a zero-duration step.\n    58→func (b *Backoff) Step() time.Duration {\n    59→\tif b == nil {\n    60→\t\treturn 0\n    61→\t}\n    62→\tvar nextDuration time.Duration\n    63→\tnextDuration, b.Duration, b.Steps = delay(b.Steps, b.Duration, b.Cap, b.Factor, b.Jitter)\n    64→\treturn nextDuration\n    65→}\n    66→\n    67→// DelayFunc returns a function that will compute the next interval to\n    68→// wait given the arguments in b. It does not mutate the original backoff\n    69→// but the function is safe to use only from a single goroutine.\n    70→func (b Backoff) DelayFunc() DelayFunc {\n    71→\tsteps := b.Steps\n    72→\tduration := b.Duration\n    73→\tcap := b.Cap\n    74→\tfactor := b.Factor\n    75→\tjitter := b.Jitter\n    76→\n    77→\treturn func() time.Duration {\n    78→\t\tvar nextDuration time.Duration\n    79→\t\t// jitter is applied per step and is not cumulative over multiple steps\n    80→\t\tnextDuration, duration, steps = delay(steps, duration, cap, factor, jitter)\n    81→\t\treturn nextDuration\n    82→\t}\n    83→}\n    84→\n    85→// Timer returns a timer implementation appropriate to this backoff's parameters\n    86→// for use with wait functions.\n    87→func (b Backoff) Timer() Timer {\n    88→\tif b.Steps > 1 || b.Jitter != 0 {\n    89→\t\treturn &variableTimer{new: internalClock.NewTimer, fn: b.DelayFunc()}\n    90→\t}\n    91→\tif b.Duration > 0 {\n    92→\t\treturn &fixedTimer{new: internalClock.NewTicker, interval: b.Duration}\n    93→\t}\n    94→\treturn newNoopTimer()\n    95→}\n    96→\n    97→// delay implements the core delay algorithm used in this package.\n    98→func delay(steps int, duration, cap time.Duration, factor, jitter float64) (_ time.Duration, next time.Duration, nextSteps int) {\n    99→\t// when steps is non-positive, do not alter the base duration\n   100→\tif steps < 1 {\n   101→\t\tif jitter > 0 {\n   102→\t\t\treturn Jitter(duration, jitter), duration, 0\n   103→\t\t}\n   104→\t\treturn duration, duration, 0\n   105→\t}\n   106→\tsteps--\n   107→\n   108→\t// calculate the next step's interval\n   109→\tif factor != 0 {\n   110→\t\tnext = time.Duration(float64(duration) * factor)\n   111→\t\tif cap > 0 && next > cap {\n   112→\t\t\tnext = cap\n   113→\t\t\tsteps = 0\n   114→\t\t}\n   115→\t} else {\n   116→\t\tnext = duration\n   117→\t}\n   118→\n   119→\t// add jitter for this step\n   120→\tif will return the appropriate next interval to\n   129→// wait. Every resetInterval the backoff parameters are reset to their initial state.\n   130→// This method is safe to invoke from multiple goroutines, but all calls will advance\n   131→// the backoff state when Factor is set. If Factor is zero, this method is the same as\n   132→// invoking b.DelayFunc() since Steps has no impact without Factor. If resetInterval is\n   133→// zero no backoff will be performed as the same calling DelayFunc with a zero factor\n   134→// and steps.\n   135→func (b Backoff) DelayWithReset(c clock.Clock, resetInterval time.Duration) DelayFunc {\n   136→\tif b.Factor <= 0 {\n   137→\t\treturn b.DelayFunc()\n   138→\t}\n   139→\tif resetInterval <= 0 {\n   140→\t\tb.Steps = 0\n   141→\t\tb.Factor = 0\n loops until stop channel is closed, running f every period.\n   198→//\n   199→// If jitterFactor is positive, the period is jittered before every run of f.\n   200→// If jitterFactor is not positive, the period is unchanged and not jittered.\n   201→//\n   202→// If sliding is true, the period is computed after f runs. If it is false then\n   203→// period includes the runtime for f.\n   204→//\n   205→// Close stopCh to stop. f may not be invoked if stop channel is already\n   206→// closed. If it is false then\n   239→// period includes the runtime for f.\n   240→func BackoffUntilWithContext(ctx context.Context, f func(ctx context.Context), backoff BackoffManager, sliding bool) {\n   241→\tvar t clock.Timer\n   242→\tfor {\n   243→\t\tselect {\n   244→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   245→\t\t\treturn\n   246→\t\tdefault:\n   247→\t\t}\n   248→\n   249→\t\tif !sliding {\n   250→\t\t\tt = 259→\t\t\tt = backoff.Backoff()\n   260→\t\t}\n   261→\n   262→\t\t// NOTE: b/c there is no priority selection in golang\n   263→\t\t// it is possible for this to race, meaning we could\n   264→\t\t// trigger t.C and stopCh, and t.C select falls through.\n   265→\t\t// In order to mitigate we re-check stopCh at the beginning\n   266→\t\t// of every loop to prevent extra executions of f().\n   267→\t\tselect {\n   268→\t\tcase <-ctx.Done():\n   269→\t\t\tif !t.Stop() {\n   270→\t\t\t\t<-t.C()\n   271→\t\t\t}\n   272→\t\t\treturn\n   273→\t\tcase <-t.C():\n   274→\t\t}\n   275→\t}\n   276→}\n   277→\n   278→// backoffManager provides simple backoff behavior in a threadsafe manner to a caller.\n   279→type backoffManager struct {\n   280→\tbackoff        Backoff\n   281→\tinitialBackoff Backoff\n   282→\tresetInterval  time.Duration\n   283→\n   284→\tclock clock.Clock\n   285→\n   286→\tlock      sync.Mutex\n   287→\tlastStart time.Time\n   288→\ttimer     clock.Timer\n   289→}\n   290→\n   291→// Step returns the expected next duration to wait.\n   292→func (b *backoffManager) Step() time.Duration {\n   293→\tb.lock.Lock()\n   294→\tdefer b.lock.Unlock()\n   295→\n   296→\tswitch {\n   297→\tcase b.resetInterval == 0:\n   298→\t\tb.backoff = b.initialBackoff\n   299→\tcase b.clock.Now().Sub(b.lastStart) > b.resetInterval:\n   300→\t\tb.backoff = b.initialBackoff\n   301→\t\tb.lastStart = b.clock.Now()\n   302→\t}\n   303→\treturn b.backoff.Step()\n   304→}\n   305→\n   306→// Backoff implements BackoffManager.Backoff, it returns a timer so caller can block on the timer\n   307→// for exponential backoff. The returned timer must be drained before calling Backoff() the second\n   308→// time.\n   309→func (b *backoffManager) Backoff() clock.Timer {\n   310→\tb.lock.Lock()\n   311→\tdefer b.lock.Unlock()\n   312→\tif b.timer == nil {\n   313→\t\tb.timer = b.clock.NewTimer(b.Step())\n   314→\t} else {\n   315→\t\tb.timer.Reset(b.Step())\n   316→\t}\n   317→\treturn b.timer\n   318→}\n   319→\n   320→// Timer returns a new Timer instance that shares the clock and the reset behavior with all other\n   321→// timers.\n   322→func (b *backoffManager) Timer() Timer {\n   323→\treturn DelayFunc(b.Step).Timer(b.clock)\n   324→}\n   325→\n   326→// BackoffManager manages backoff with a particular scheme based on its underlying implementation.\n   327→type BackoffManager interface {\n   328→\t// Backoff returns a shared clock.Timer that is Reset on every invocation. This method is not\n   329→\t// safe for use from multiple threads. It returns a timer for backoff, and caller shall backoff\n   330→\t// until Timer.C() drains. If the second Backoff() is called before the timer from the first\n   331→\t// Backoff() call finishes, the first timer will NOT be drained and result in undetermined\n   332→\t// behavior.\n   333→\tBackoff() clock.Timer\n   334→}\n   335→\n   336→// Deprecated: Will be removed when the legacy polling functions are removed.\n   337→type exponentialBackoffManagerImpl struct {\n   338→\tbackoff              *Backoff\n   339→\tbackoffTimer         clock.Timer\n   340→\tlastBackoffStart     time.Time\n   341→\tinitialBackoff       time.Duration\n   342→\tbackoffResetDuration time.Duration\n   343→\tclock                clock.Clock\n   344→}\n   345→\n   346→// NewExponentialBackoffManager returns a manager for managing exponential backoff. Each backoff is jittered and\n   347→// backoff will not exceed the given max. If the backoff is not called within resetDuration, the backoff is reset.\n   348→// This backoff manager is used to reduce load during upstream unhealthiness.\n   349→//\n   350→// Deprecated: Will be removed when the legacy Poll methods are removed. Callers should construct a\n   351→// Backoff struct, use DelayWithReset() to get a DelayFunc that periodically resets itself, and then\n   352→// invoke Timer() when calling wait.BackoffUntil.\n   353→//\n   354→// Instead of:\n   355→//\n   356→//\tbm := wait.NewExponentialBackoffManager(init, max, reset, factor, jitter, clock)\n   357→//\t...\n   358→//\twait.BackoffUntil(..., bm.Backoff, float64(init))), // now a required argument\n   366→//\t  Factor:   factor,\n   367→//\t  Jitter:   jitter,\n   368→//\t}.DelayWithReset(reset, clock)\n   369→//\twait.BackoffUntil(..., delayFn.Timer(), ...)\n   370→func NewExponentialBackoffManager(initBackoff, maxBackoff, resetDuration time.Duration, backoffFactor, jitter float64, c clock.Clock) BackoffManager {\n   371→\treturn &exponentialBackoffManagerImpl{\n   372→\t\tbackoff: &Backoff{\n   373→\t\t\tDuration: initBackoff,\n   374→\t\t\tFactor:   backoffFactor,\n   375→\t\t\tJitter:   jitter,\n   376→\n   377→\t\t\t// the c.Now(),\n   385→\t\tbackoffResetDuration: resetDuration,\n   386→\t\tclock:                c,\n   387→\t}\n   388→}\n   389→\n   390→func (b *exponentialBackoffManagerImpl) getNextBackoff() time.Duration {\n   391→\tif b.clock.Now().Sub(b.lastBackoffStart) > b.backoffResetDuration {\n   392→\t\tb.backoff.Steps = math.MaxInt32\n   393→\t\tb.backoff.Duration = b.initialBackoff\n   394→\t}\n   395→\tb.lastBackoffStart = b.clock.Now()\n   396→\treturn b.backoff.Step()\n   397→}\n   398→\n   399→// Backoff implements BackoffManager.Backoff, it returns a timer so caller can block on the timer for exponential backoff.\n   400→// The returned timer must be drained before calling Backoff() the second time\n   401→func (b *exponentialBackoffManagerImpl) Backoff() clock.Timer {\n   402→\tif b.backoffTimer == nil {\n   403→\t\tb.backoffTimer = b.clock.NewTimer(b.getNextBackoff())\n   404→\t} else {\n   405→\t\tb.backoffTimer.Reset(b.getNextBackoff())\n   406→\t}\n   407→\treturn b.backoffTimer\n   408→}\n   409→\n   410→// Deprecated: Will be removed when the legacy polling functions are removed.\n   411→type jitteredBackoffManagerImpl struct {\n   412→\tclock       b,\n\t\tinitialBackoff: b,\n\t\tresetInterval:  resetInterval,\n\n\t\tclock:     c,\n\t\tlastStart: c.Now(),\n\t\ttimer:     nil,\n\t}).Step\n}\n\n// Until loops until stop channel is closed,
